\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Mtc\_CallDbGetIpCallBreakOut()}{Mtc\_CallDbGetIpCallBreakOut()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily Z\+F\+U\+NC Z\+B\+O\+OL Mtc\+\_\+\+Call\+Db\+Get\+Ip\+Call\+Break\+Out (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{Z\+F\+U\+N\+C\+\_\+\+V\+O\+ID}]{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Get a device in R\+C\+S-\/\+AA mode whether it can initiate Voice calls even if the recipient user does not show service capability for voice calls. It is required in devices that can function in R\+C\+S-\/\+AA mode. It will not be instantiated if the service provider does not support the best effort IP Voice Call service. 


\begin{DoxyRetVals}{Return values}
{\em Z\+T\+R\+UE} & Indicates an IP Voice Call cannot be initiated if an error (480/404) is returned to a request for the recipient user\textquotesingle{}s service capabilities or service capabilities do not indicate the support of IP Voice Call. \\
\hline
{\em Z\+F\+A\+L\+SE} & Indicates an IP Voice Call to be initiated even if an error (480/404) is returned to a request for the recipient user?s service capabilities or service capabilities do not indicate the support of IP Voice Call.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyRetVals}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\mbox{\hyperlink{mtc__call__db_8h_ad284d02ce5283df94b59624c3348b8ea}{Mtc\+\_\+\+Call\+Db\+Set\+Ip\+Call\+Break\+Out}}

Get the Ue authorization for user to use best effort IP Video Call service. 


\begin{DoxyRetVals}{Return values}
{\em 0} & Indicates that best effort IP Video Call service is disabled. \\
\hline
{\em 1} & Indicates that best effort IP Video Call service is enabled for non-\/3\+G\+P\+P/non-\/3\+G\+P\+P2 access only (e.\+g. Wi-\/\+Fi, x\+D\+SL). \\
\hline
{\em 2} & Indicates that best effort IP Video Call service is enabled for ~\newline
 non-\/3\+G\+P\+P/non-\/3\+G\+P\+P2 access (e.\+g. Wi-\/\+Fi, x\+D\+SL) and for L\+TE access. \\
\hline
{\em 3} & Indicates that best effort IP Video Call service is enabled for ~\newline
 non-\/3\+G\+P\+P/non-\/3\+G\+P\+P2 access (e.\+g. Wi-\/\+Fi, x\+D\+SL) and for L\+T\+E/\+H\+S\+PA access. \\
\hline
{\em 4} & Indicates that best effort IP Video Call service is enabled for A\+NY access except 2G access.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyRetVals}

Get an R\+C\+S-\/\+CS device whether it can initiate a best effort IP Video Call upgrade without first tearing down the CS voice call. It is required in devices that can function in R\+C\+S-\/\+CS mode. It is will not be instantiated if the service provider does not support the IP Video Call service. 


\begin{DoxyRetVals}{Return values}
{\em Z\+T\+R\+UE} & Indicates a best effort IP Video Call can be initiated even before the CS voice call is torn down. \\
\hline
{\em Z\+F\+A\+L\+SE} & Indicates a best effort IP Video Call can only be initiated once the CS voice call has been torn down.\\
\hline
